 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g116170g01a02.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g116170dsp02.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Time is Running Out! </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>PLEASE VOTE TODAY </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Goldman Sachs Trust
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">The Special Meeting of Shareholders has been adjourned for a second time to April&nbsp;16, 2021, due to the lack of shareholder participation.
It is critical that your voice be heard on this very important proposal concerning making a change to your fund&#146;s subclassification from &#145;diversified&#146; to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#145;non-diversified&#146;.</FONT> The Board
has unanimously voted to approve this change, subject to shareholder approval. The change cannot take place without the support of shareholders like you. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>According to our records, we have not received your vote! </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Management recommends a FOR vote on the proposal, however, voting in any manner will help us reach quorum and stop any further outreach concerning this
meeting. </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">It is important that we receive your vote prior to April 16<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> because it will
help to avoid adjourning the meeting further and having to spend additional money soliciting your votes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>If you have any questions or would like
to vote, </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>please call the number listed below: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:24pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">833-934-2733</FONT></FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">Your vote is important no matter the size of your fund holdings. Please vote promptly so your vote can be received prior to the April&nbsp;16, 2021
Special Meeting of Shareholders. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>The funds have made it very easy for you to vote. </B></P>
